<UserId.>111164137286405704254</UserId.><Name>Barb Fischer San Diego Real Estate Broker</Name><Time>1560209872229<//Time><Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
Really enjoyable dining experience in a pleasant part of downtown. 4th floor, so when the sun sets on the west-caving balcony you'll want a hat so that you can actually see. without getting blinded.  A new building is going up right across the street, and it will block half of the view, but look to the left and right and you'll still get a good vista. Also, there is a long row of seating which works well for couples, but not so good for conversation with larger parties. Unique choices of foods, for example an appetizer of bacon-wrapped dates. There is plenty to choose from for special diets. Salmon was fantastic and came with tons of veggies and quinoa.<//review>

< text>
This store has a great selection of party decorations and supplies. It has a limited selection of food. Everything else is standard.

The only caution I'd relate is that if you buy party supplies and anything happens so that the party is cancelled and you have to return items (for exchange only), you don't get store credit to use whenever. You can only exchange it right then and no food items (that part wasn't explained when I asked before I bought the items). I volunteered to do all of the legwork for a work baby shower, which was cancelled. I had to make returns to a number of stores, including a 99 Cent Store that had a better exchange policy and similar products.

I will buy personal items at a Dollar Tree without reservation. I will buy future bulk party items at a 99 Cent store.< /text>

<user_id>101492315302140664532</user_id><user_name>Gina Ortiz</user_name>< Date>
1555883236758</Date>
< rating>
5< /rating>
< review>
This is the BEST storage place I've ever used (and I've used a LOT).
This compound is HUGE. So much bigger than you can see from the outside. It's very well maintained, VERY clean (spotless, in fact), secure, and really convenient to access.

IT'S ALSO A UHAUL LOCATION! You can sign up for a storage unit AND rent a truck at the same time! $19.95 for a standard truck or cargo van? I am IN!

BUILDING: It's conveniently located right off the freeway and Chapman Ave. The building itself is incredibly clean and secure, and the interiors all have wide hallways, bright lighting, and fire sprinkler systems all along the halls. There is no trash or junk anywhere, they have a huge variety of unit sizes and shapes, and it's also air conditioned!

SECURITY: Entry into the property has a coded-access gate and security cameras everywhere. When you go inside to sign up, you'll be able to see their security monitors which display every nook 'n cranny of the property. The manager is onsite 24/7 and watches the property at all times. I don't think I've ever seen a storage facility that was more secure than this one.

ACCESSIBILITY: You can pull your vehicle right up to your unit if you're on the ground floor. My unit is on the 2nd floor, so I pulled right up to the elevator door, literally 3 steps away from it. The elevator is spacious and clean, and actually works. Load-in took only minutes because my unit was so close to the elevator, I was in and out very quickly. The parking/ loading area is circular, so you can get back out without having to back up.

STAFF: Super-friendly and cool (funny, actually). Sheila (the manager), made the sign-up process a breeze. She's fast and efficient, and explained everything very thoroughly so I wasn't hit with any surprises. She'll get you in and out in just a few minutes.

FEES: Very reasonable, in fact I got 50% discount for the first 3 months because they're having an online special. You must make your reservation online, but that was also super-easy. Just so you know, they strongly recommend using their special circular locks, because they are very difficult to cut through. Be prepared to spend an extra $12 on the lock (but you keep it).

OTHER THINGS TO KNOW: You MUST buy insurance in order to rent a unit here. It's mandatory but cheap ($9), and it's good coverage. Last but not least, they do charge a $25 administration fee, which is kind of a bummer, but it is a one-time charge. All and all I saved money, since this place is still less expensive than most of the others in the neighborhood. The cleanliness and security make it worth every penny. I'm really happy I found this place, because it's so close to my house that I can pop in to pick up/drop off stuff so easily. I just wish I would've known about it sooner! I highly recommend this company!< /review>

<user>102911018563516196880</user>< user_name>
Eric Eltzholtz< /user_name>
<time>1621218406846<//time><rating>5</rating>< Review>
Super cool Temecula Winery, here's why my wife and I love it. 1. After years of being members at some other local wineries, that have become too overcrowded we love that Masia is slightly off the beaten path. 2. The wine club membership for local Temeculites is un-equaled and I love the private wine club lounge. 3. The views of the Eastern Temecula Valley along with the afternoon coastal clouds creeping over Mt. Palomar are breathtaking. 4. The staff is friendly,  knowledgable and easygoing. 5. The Brut, I'm so sorry there are other Temecula wineries making a name off of sparkling wine...they don't even come close in comparison. 5. They have a relationship with sister winery Danza Del Sol. Enjoy!<//Review>

Nice smaller winery.  Excellent views.  No food, unless they have a food truck, which means you are allowed to bring your own food onto the property.  The view that they have is amazing.  The Wine Club also has its own room and patio on the weekends.  This is a great benefit if you come on the weekends.  Service has been hit and miss.  They also have entertainment on the weekends.  I can't say that I am a fan of all of their wines, but they do have some have some excellent varieties.  This is owned by Danza del Sol and they use the same wine maker, but it is not the same wine.<//Review>

< Text>
I work at Cal and this place is on the way from home. I've given this place about 10 second chances and am finally done. Generic, Dunkin Doughnuts style bagels (aka just bread in the shape of a bagel) and the employees are straight up incompetent. I assume there is zero effort put in by the manager, if they even have one. On multiple occasions, I've ordered a half dozen bagels, paid, and watched as others behind me in line ordered the same/more bagels and had their order filled while I politely stood there waiting. Zero organization among the employees. Ordered a breakfast sandwich today, and they literally piled the egg, sausage, and room temperature cheese onto a bagel and gave it to me without even heating it up. Speed is great, but I'm willing to wait more than 30 seconds if it means I can actually have a warm food item. Never coming here again.<//Text>

I ordered a pastry and a drip coffee, and before I paid, he warned me that only two flavors of coffee were available  (it was 2:45 and they close at 4). Considering I have come in before 11am and had every container empty besides decaf, I appreciated him wanting to make sure they had the flavor I wanted. The woman in line behind me ordered bagels and shmear, and he showed her the same courtesy and told her that, if she didn't see the flavor of shmear she wanted, he would go in the back and get it for her. And he did. When I come back to Noah's, it will be for Markel.< /Review></record>
